## Text Elements
#sacu1 ^4kQG4nJZ

Def. (sequence): function a: N⟶R. ∴ maps natural numbers
to real numbers. Notation: a(1), a(2),... or a₁ a₂, ..., aₙ, ... Order of
elements matter, ∴ exchanging changes the sequence ^r0joUOjp

Examples ^uuPz7GQB

def ^4AOkQ83u

aₙ is bounded below if E m<=aₙ V n ^QdTTWF7Q

aₙ is bounded above if E M>=aₙ V n ^aRt6pwgJ

def ^Zi7NSRUK

def ^m1lXQ696

aₙ is bounded if above ^ below ^CnOxBqzh

def ^YEfJhWrT

aₙ is increasing if
 aₙ₊₁>=aₙ V n ^Feg38ajz

aₙ is decreasing if
 aₙ₊₁<=aₙ V n ^je764MLp

def ^8Y6Q2yrf

aₙ is monotone ^obcDR4Zu

lower bounded (m=2), 
monotonically increasing ^U7p1urbp

bounded (m=0, M=1), 
monotonically decreasing ^QjuouVVF

bounded (m=0=M), 
monotonically decreasing ^ increasing  ^oSh2vMkh

def ^zJbcp2If

aₙ converges to L if V 
ε>0 E nₖ s.t. ε>|L-aₙ| (n>=nₖ)
(we can choose whatever small ε and 
will find an index nₖ where aₙ-L is <ε) ^d2uUR1WV

Example ^JGs4lU6D

def ^aPCZvp7D

aₙ diverges to ꝏ if V 
M E nₖ s.t. M<aₙ (n>=nₖ) ^jM2IOb3G

aₙ diverges to -ꝏ if V 
m E nₖ s.t. m>aₙ (n>=nₖ) ^IjKJCp5j

remark ^Eb953PHd

sequences can be represented as functions f(x)=aₙ for n<=x<n+1, n=1,2,3,... ^pGoeLdm1

why? ^EbPsaU3j

calculate easier
 lim aₙ as n⟶ꝏ ^I6PwHNKC

brings back
theorems
from limits ^PugL3doj

aₙ⟶L ^ bₙ⟶M ^gnQjOBtV

aₙ+bₙ⟶L+M ^9J4HDFv9

aₙ.bₙ⟶L.M ^fMRyW3Hz

aₙ/bₙ⟶L/M
(if possible
to divide) ^WXxDx5fP

Two Carabinieri: aₙ⟶L ^ bₙ⟶L,
 ^ aₙ<=cₙ<=bₙ. ⟶ cₙ⟶L ^aHDDhGU0
